Local News

Party Teacher Qualification Review Committee 97

Yang Xiao's First Batch of Qualified Personnel

A Total of Ninety-Nine People

Officially Announced Today

The City's Party Ideology Teacher Qualification Review Committee has just completed the process of revealing the first batch of ninety-five Party Ideology teachers of all levels who have been approved for qualification. The procedures for receiving certificates are ready and the list will be announced in the newspapers starting today, and the procedures for receiving certificates will be announced as follows:

▲Procedures for Receiving Qualification Certificates: (1) You must bring the following three items to receive the qualification certificate: A. Your personal seal, B. Receipt from this committee, C. A stamp (3 jiao for middle school, 1 jiao for primary school). (2) After the committee verifies that the review form is correct, it will notify the training section of the Municipal Party Department to complete the registration and issue the certificate of eligibility. (3) The documents submitted will be returned upon presentation of the committee receipt. (4) The certificate recipient will then go to the training section of the Municipal Party Department to fill out the registration form (not required for those not in this city). (6) The training section of the Municipal Party Department will issue a Shanghai Party Ideology Teacher Registration Certificate, indicating a direct relationship with the Shanghai Municipal Party Department. (7) Those who reside outside the city and are unable to come to the committee in person to receive the certificate must attach the following: 1. A paper with their personal seal, 2. Receipt from this committee, 3. A stamp, 4. Required registered postage, and the certificate will be mailed to them.

Also, it is heard that the second batch, totaling one hundred and eighty-five people, has been approved by the Municipal Executive Committee at its meeting on the 7th and certificates are being prepared. It is expected that they will also be announced around the middle of this month. From now on, all levels of schools will only employ Party Ideology teachers and instructors who hold a review certificate or a registered qualification certificate from the Review Qualification Committee. All previously issued qualification certificates, etc., will be invalid. The committee has also issued a notice and a letter to the Municipal Education Bureau to verify this.

The Municipal Education Bureau is Ordered to Conduct a Supplementary Screening Examination for Students of the Former Middle School Department of Labor University 98

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau, in order to conduct a supplementary screening examination for students of the former Middle School Department of the National Labor University, issued a notice yesterday stating, "This bureau previously received an order from the ministry to conduct a screening examination for students of the former Middle School Department of the National Labor University and issued transfer certificates to those who passed. Now, the Ministry of Education has ordered that students of the former Middle School Department of Labor University who have not been screened are allowed to register for a supplementary screening examination, provided that the bureau verifies that the students were indeed unable to arrive for the examination due to flooding in various locations. Therefore, it is decided that September 18th and 19th will be the registration dates and September 25th and 26th will be the examination dates. Students of the school who have not been screened should come to the bureau to register within the specified dates and submit two recent half-length photos (4 inches) to be reviewed and issued admission tickets to enter the examination hall. This notice is urgently announced to the public.

Qingguang's Impressive Performance 108

Defeated Hujiang 36-30 Last Night

Jinan Won Against Military Academy in Overtime

Score: 55 to 52

The Qingguang basketball team defeated the powerful Hujiang team 36-30 in the second act of the disaster relief basketball game last night. The score was close, and the performance was excellent, especially Qingguang's performance in the second half, which was particularly impressive. In the first game, Jinan won against the Military Academy 55-52 in overtime.

Jinan Wins Against Military Academy 109

The Military Academy performed very well in the first half, winning 26-17 against Jinan. After the second half, with the score at 42-31, Jinan gradually caught up, ending in a 44-44 tie. There was a ten-minute overtime. In the first five minutes, Jinan won 50-46. The Military Academy added four points, and it was a tie again. The atmosphere was tense. Jinan finally won 55-52. The referee was Qu Hongren.

Qingguang Triumphs Over Hujiang 110

The battle between Qingguang and Hujiang, a sequel to their previous encounter, saw both teams with high hopes in the City Games. Last night, Qingguang steadily improved after a slow start, ultimately winning with a score of 36 to 30, a truly remarkable feat. The referee was Shao Ji.

▲The tension of the match was such that the difference between the scores of the two teams was usually only two or three points, a very close margin. Initially, the five young tiger generals of Hujiang scored seven points in one go. Within ten minutes, Qingguang caught up, making the score seven to nine. Hujiang then deployed its university team. Qingguang then evened the score at fourteen to fourteen. In the first half, Hujiang narrowly won by two points, sixteen to fourteen. In the second half, Hujiang's youth team scored again, leaving only Lu Zhong'en. Qingguang added Lu Dazhen, which became a turning point. After several ties, each at twenty-six, Qingguang then surpassed Hujiang from then on, sailing smoothly to victory with a score of thirty-six to thirty.

▲Qingguang's prowess was evident in Tan Dahua's undiminished power, with his brilliant moments visible. His individual skills are rare. The defense and offense of Zhang Jinxiang, the defender, were truly his contribution last night. Xu Kepei's shooting accuracy was slightly lacking, and the addition of Lu Dazhen was a major factor in Qingguang's turnaround.

▲Hujiang's triple substitution: Hujiang first used its middle school team for ten minutes, then its university team for the rest of the first half. In the second half, the middle school team reappeared, leaving only Lu Zhong'en. The three forwards of the middle school team were incredibly agile, with their shooting skills particularly outstanding. The university team's forwards were completely ineffective. The substitution occurred mid-game, which was one of the reasons for the loss. Furthermore, the three young men gradually exhausted their energy, leading to their falling behind, which was also a significant failure. In terms of performance, they were by no means weak.

Chinese National Amateur Athletic Federation Corrects National Record 112

800-Meter Relay

A notice from the Chinese National Amateur Athletic Federation states: Upon investigation, the previously announced national track and field record for the 800-meter relay (1 minute 37 and 5/10 seconds, set by the Northeast University team) was actually bettered by the Chinese team in the China-U.S. athletic meet in Shanghai. Therefore, the correction is as follows:

800-meter relay time: 1 minute 35 and 1/5 seconds, Chinese team (Zhou Ende, Zhou Zhaoyuan, Mai Guozhen, Zhong Lianji), set on May 10, 1920, at the China-U.S. athletic meet in Shanghai.

The Question of the Top Ten Tennis Players in China - Lin Baohua Did Not Boast About Being Number One 116

His Respected Father, Mr. Lin Shufen, Writes to Clarify

Mr. Lin's Original Intention Was to Encourage Young Rising Talents

Mr. Liu's Comments Can Be Used for Future Reference

Since this newspaper disclosed ("Mr. Liu Keng's Discussion with Mr. Lin Baohua Regarding the Rankings of the Top Ten Tennis Players in China"), people in the tennis world have paid close attention. Yesterday, the editor received a letter from Mr. Lin Shufen, the respected father of Lin Baohua, clarifying that Lin Baohua did not boast about being number one. Moreover, the focus of his discussion was on how recent masters have improved their techniques, with the sincere intention of encouraging young rising talents, and with no malice or favoritism involved. It is noted that the Chinese National Amateur Athletic Federation will invite domestic and foreign masters to gather in Shanghai for performances before this year's National Games. At that time, the rankings of the top ten players may be officially produced. As Mr. Liu Keng's expressed his views in response to Mr. Lin's discussion of the rankings of the top ten players, and since Mr. Lin did not intend to compile a list of the top ten masters, Mr. Liu's comments can be reserved for future reference. The original letter from his respected father, Lin Shufen, is attached below:

To the Sports Editor of Shen Bao,

Respectfully,

I read yesterday's report in your newspaper about Mr. Liu Keng's conversation with a reporter from the Shih Pao regarding Chinese masters. I was also present. Without any malice or favoritism, and knowing that even the best sun does not shine for long, I sincerely wanted to encourage talented young people so that they can restore China's reputation in tennis at the 10th Far Eastern Championship Games. There was no intention to slight Mr. Liu, Mr. Jiang, or other masters. I hope that national players with a generous and chivalrous spirit will not hesitate to sacrifice a little to encourage the enthusiasm and interest of rising talents.

(2) When talking with the Shih Pao reporter, Baohua did not mention his own name, so how could he have been intending to demean others? He was actually trying to guess which young, promising talents in China might have the opportunity to represent China in the future. He was not aware of those who were in Shanghai or abroad. This was not intended to compile a list of the top ten masters. Generally speaking, there are many tennis enthusiasts in Shanghai and elsewhere. If he talked with Yuliuke late at night about how the techniques of recent masters have improved, it was not with any malice or favoritism. Moreover, Baohua did not boast about being number one, so if Mr. Liu put himself in his place, would he not have said the same?

(3) Mr. Jiang's skill and experience have made great contributions to the country on many occasions, and he is praised by everyone. It would be shocking to place him below Mr. Zheng, but Mr. Zheng's recent improvement in tennis skills is indeed surprising. I believe you have also heard that Mr. Zhao Jiajun defeated Canadian Davis Cup player Mr. Duff in Lushan Guling. I suppose private discussions are also subject to criticism.

Sincerely,

Lin Shufen

Yesterday (the 9th) was the 36th anniversary of the Premier's first uprising. The Shanghai Special City Party Headquarters specially convened representatives from all sectors of the city to hold a commemorative meeting at the auditorium on the third floor of the City Party Headquarters. Over 800 representatives from various agencies, groups, schools, and party headquarters at all levels attended. Chairman Pan Gongzhan first reported on the facts of the Premier's first uprising and the understanding and efforts that we should have. Then, Du Gang gave a speech, filled with encouragement and inspiration, which moved the listeners deeply. The details of the meeting are recorded below.

▲Meeting Order (1) All stand at attention; (2) Sing the Party song; (3) Offer the highest respect to the Party and national flag and the Premier's portrait; (4) Chairman respectfully reads the Premier's will; (5) Silent tribute; (6) Chairman's report; (7) Speech; (8) Shout slogans; (9) Adjourn.

▲Meeting Slogans (1) Continue the Premier's revolutionary spirit; (2) Continue the martyrs' spirit of sacrifice; (3) Thoroughly eradicate the Red bandits; (4) Eliminate reactionary remnants; (5) Strive for disaster relief work; (6) Support peaceful unification; (7) Complete local autonomy; (8) Implement political tutelage and construction; (9) Realize the Three People's Principles; (10) Complete the National Revolution; (11) Long live the Chinese Kuomintang; (12) Long live the Republic of China.

The National Government Disaster Relief Committee Held a General Meeting Yesterday 118

Decided to Continue Issuing 1.4 Million in Relief Funds

Passed the Addition of 17 Standing Committee Members

The Regulations of Each Group Were Handed Over to the Standing Committee for Handling

The National Government Disaster Relief Committee held its first general meeting of members yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM at the Central Bank on the Bund, adjourning at 5:10 PM. The details of the meeting are recorded below.

▲Committee Members Present The attendees included Chairman Song Ziwen, Committee Members Kong Xiangxi, Xu Shiying, Zhu Qinglan, Wang Zhen, Wang Xiaolai, Zhou Xiangxian, Cha Liangzhao, Liu Ruiheng, Zeng Rongfu, Zheng Yuxiu, Shi Liangcai, Song Hanzhang, Lin Kanghou, Zhang Gongquan, Yu Qiaqing, Zhang Yuanshan, Baker, Ma Xier, Carney, and others, totaling over 80 people.

▲Meeting Details The meeting started at 3:10 PM. Chairman Song Ziwen first reported on the work done before the establishment of the committee and the committee's future work plan. Then, Zhu Qinglan, Mr. Baker, Liu Ruiheng, Kong Xiangxi, Zhang Gongquan, and others followed with their reports. The meeting also passed the addition of 17 Chinese and foreign members to the Standing Committee. The draft rules of procedure for the committee were resolved to be decided by the Standing Committee. The meeting adjourned at 5:15 PM.

▲List of Standing Committee Members Song Ziwen, Kong Xiangxi, Xu Shiying, Zhu Qinglan, Liu Shangqing, Zhang Gongquan, Yu Qiaqing, Zeng Rongfu, Liu Ruiheng, Zheng Yuxiu, Baker, Ma Xier, Carney, Funatsu Tatsuo, Kanai Kiyoshi, Lu Benting, Ma Su,

▲Mr. Song's Report Honorable Committee Members, today is the first general meeting of this committee. I would like to take this opportunity to report to you on the official establishment of this committee and the work that has already been done. I would also like to briefly outline my humble views on the future work plan for your consideration. The severity of the disaster in the affected areas, beyond the Jianghuai River basin, need not be elaborated upon. As of today, scientific and detailed reports on the disaster situation in the disaster areas are still not available. The National Government, recognizing the seriousness of the situation, has established this committee to handle disaster relief matters and is responsible for raising large amounts of funds and purchasing large quantities of grain for disaster relief purposes. It is estimated that the committee will spend over 70 million national currency in total for disaster relief, including both cash and grain. Today, most of you, with a few exceptions, do not have much experience in disaster relief affairs. Or, the entire audience has never experienced such an unprecedented relief effort. The magnitude of this disaster is rare in history, and the relief strategies cannot be rigidly adhered to old methods, but must seek long-term measures that are adapted to the times. The questions before us today are what problems we face and what plans we should have. The victims are in urgent need of help, and all problems are complex. What we should pay attention to is that all plans should not be empty and unrealistic. Today, there are many discussions on disaster relief strategies, such as dredging the Huai River and improving the Yangtze River waterway. Their arguments are certainly appealing, but in reality, whether both are carried out simultaneously or one is carried out first, the funds required will be in the hundreds of millions. Regardless of whether this committee can obtain this huge amount of money at one time, even if the huge amount of money is fully collected, the engineering technology will not be sufficient. In the past, the United States of America suffered from floods in the Mississippi River for a long time. The cost of river management before and after was no less than hundreds of millions of dollars, but it still failed to permanently eliminate its disaster. The Mississippi River is short and small, far inferior to the Yangtze River. The manpower and financial resources spent were like that, but it still failed to make it obey. It can be seen how easy it is to talk about improving the Yangtze River waterway. So, what is the purpose of this committee? According to the results of the exchange of opinions among the groups of this committee, our answer to this question is roughly as follows: First, do our best to provide emergency relief to the victims, prioritize the distribution of food, build shelters, and prepare for sanitation and epidemic prevention. Second, wait until the floodwaters recede slightly and immediately repair the dikes to restore them to their original state. Although we have very little knowledge of water conservancy, such a large flood will cost an unlimited amount of money, and the dikes built will be extremely strong, but they will still not be able to resist this flood. This is generally recognized by various experts. Therefore, given the committee's limited financial resources, we can only plan to repair the old dikes or build new dikes so that they will not cause disasters under normal rainfall. What is said above does not mean that the National Government will never have specific and large-scale plans to dredge rivers in the future, but what this committee can do today is not enough to talk about this. Third, the committee should purchase and store grain seeds in advance, and distribute them to the victims after the floodwaters recede to be used for spring plowing next year, and at any time assist in the work of restoring farmland to its original state. We are ashamed that the above-mentioned proposals are simple, but even this simple plan is difficult for the committee's financial resources to cope with. However, we have to be down-to-earth and simplify things due to poverty, so the difficulties in this should be understood by the Chinese people. In order for the committee's work to proceed immediately, the five committee members initially appointed by the committee have assigned the directors of each group as follows: Zeng Rongpu is the director of the Investigation Group, Zhu Qinglan is the director of the Disaster Area Work Group, I will serve as the director of the Finance Group, Zhang Jiaju is the director of the Accounting and Audit Group, Yu Qiaqing is the director of the Transportation Group, Liu Ruiheng is the director of the Surgery and Hygiene Group, and Kong Xiangxi is the director of the Liaison Group. The gentlemen listed above are probably known to all of you present. When the candidates for the directors of each group were initially determined, although they all declined due to insufficient talent and ability, it was difficult to recruit responsible people for a time. After repeated persuasion, they each agreed to take responsibility. The detailed list of each group has long been issued by the committee and disclosed in various newspapers. Secondly, we should solemnly express our gratitude to all Chinese and foreigners who have generously donated funds. Although the government is doing its best to raise funds, the public funds obtained are still insufficient. To relieve the crisis and alleviate the difficulties, we rely on the support of the masses. This time, in the country, the amount of donations from groups and individuals received by this committee and other disaster relief organizations is unprecedented, and the courage to donate is rare. Abroad, even in the midst of economic depression and sluggish industries, the assistance and sympathy from all parties has not diminished. Within the first week after the establishment of the committee, the donations received totaled 1,044,580 yuan and 61,794 taels of silver (the amount of silver in this newspaper on the 3rd was incorrect, and is corrected here). Thereafter, there have been many successive donations. It is estimated that private donations will still reach several million yuan, and it is hoped that they will come in steadily. The Finance Group, Accounting and Audit Group, and Disaster Area Work Group have proposed that, in addition to the 1 million yuan in relief funds temporarily allocated by the National Government last time, 1.4 million yuan should be immediately allocated to the following provinces: Hubei 400,000 yuan, Anhui 300,000 yuan, Jiangsu 300,000 yuan, Jiangxi 100,000 yuan, Hunan 100,000 yuan, Henan 100,000 yuan, and medical expenses 100,000 yuan, totaling 1.4 million yuan. In addition, this committee has also received a donation of food and supplies worth 300,000 Japanese yen from the Japan Flood Relief Association, and it is now planned to distribute the items as follows: (1) Rice and flour should be distributed in Hubei. (2) Blankets and milk should be stored and used by the Medical Group. After my report, I would like to invite the Director of the Disaster Area Work Group, the Director of the Health and Epidemic Prevention Group, the Director of the Accounting and Audit Group, and the representatives of the Engineering Department to give a simple report on the work of their respective departments. Before I finish my report, I would like to offer a few more words for our common encouragement. The public words of Chinese and foreign disaster relief experts say that the difficulty of disaster relief is not on the day when the disaster first forms, but after the disaster continues and the disaster victims are in the most difficult situation. It is not in the extremely enthusiastic period of the disaster, but on the day when the disaster sound gradually subsides. When the disaster first forms, the victims may have a little surplus grain, and the enthusiastic calls from the society and the enthusiastic donations from local charitable organizations are enough to save the hungry and drowning for a time. However, as time passes, autumn ends and winter comes, the days are cold and the nights are long, and ice and snow cover the ground. The voice of social disaster relief has gradually subsided, and the donations from local charities have been almost exhausted. Only at this time is the function of this committee the most important and the disaster victims' hope for us is the most urgent. Therefore, given the status of this committee today, if we save a little surplus money in the early stage of disaster relief, people will regard it as having other intentions. However, if we exhaust all our resources and use them all at one time today, people may later criticize us for being shortsighted. After repeated deliberations, we have first drafted an estimate of expenses for the next six months for your consideration: (Disaster Relief Expenses Estimate) Wheat (relief and work relief) 37,500,000 yuan, transportation costs (including warehouse, insurance, and packaging fees) 12,000,000 yuan, disaster relief work expenses (including dike construction materials, equipment, workshops, supervision, and temporary shelters) 10,000,000 yuan, winter clothing for disaster victims 3,500,000 yuan, health work 1,000,000 yuan, emergency expenses already paid 1,000,000 yuan, reserve fund 5,000,000 yuan, totaling 70,000,000 yuan.

▲Gong County Begs for Relief The National Government Disaster Relief Committee received a report yesterday that the flood in Gong County, Henan Province, has spread over 600 square miles, and about 10,000 people are homeless. There is an urgent need for relief grain and medicine to be transported to the area to meet the emergency needs.

▲Denmark Donates Medicine Chairman Song of the National Government Disaster Relief Committee announced yesterday that the Danish government has donated a large number of typhoid and cholera (cholera) vaccines for the use of refugees in the disaster area. The Relief Committee has gratefully received and thanked them. The telegram was sent by the Danish Minister to China, Mr. Gao Fuke, and contained a telegram of condolences for the disaster, which stated: To Chairman Song of the Disaster Relief Committee, the people of our country are saddened by the disastrous flood in the Yangtze River basin. Our government is willing to provide assistance to the disaster within its capacity. I have been specially instructed to inquire whether your disaster area currently needs typhoid and cholera vaccines to prevent epidemics. It is now planned that the Danish Serum Institute will provide typhoid and cholera vaccines for 100,000 people. This medicine can be shipped out of Siberia within two weeks after consultation with Dr. Madsen, the director of the institute and chairman of the Health Committee of the League of Nations. Please reply immediately and indicate the place of arrival.

▲Japanese Personnel Coming to China The National Government Disaster Relief Committee has learned that Duke Tokugawa, President of the Japanese Red Cross Society, has now dispatched representatives to China to express condolences for the flood disaster and bring 30,000 Japanese yen in relief funds.

The Municipal Executive Committee Issues its Political Stance 119

Replies to General Commander Chiang and Deputy Commander Zhang by Telegram

Calling for the Cessation of Civil War to Save the Nation from Danger

The Municipal Party Headquarters Executive Committee has been receiving telegrams from General Commander Chiang and Deputy Commander Zhang for several days. Yesterday, it was reported to the meeting and it was resolved to reply separately by telegram. It is understood that these telegrams have already been drafted and sent. The content is quite important. The original text is recorded below:

▲Reply to General Commander Chiang by Telegram To Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, National Government, Nanjing,

Your telegram expressing love for peace and concern for the nation, taking responsibility with courage and reprimanding yourself with utmost sincerity, has deeply moved and inspired us. In recent years, our country has been plagued by successive rebellions, frequent wars, rampant Red bandits, and foreign aggression. In addition, water, drought, hail, and successive disasters have occurred. The melons of Huangtai are picked again and again, and the national crisis has reached its extreme. In these difficult times, all of us who are alive and have a sense of righteousness should cut our hair and put on our armor, unite as one, and work together to save the nation. We should pool our wisdom and efforts to reverse the decline. If there are still disloyal party members, shameless politicians, and domineering soldiers who only know their own selfish interests and disregard the happiness of the whole, attempting to cause chaos and recklessly starting wars, not hesitating to inflict suffering on the disaster victims and destroy the foundation of the nation, then they are traitors to the party and the country, and everyone has the right to punish them. We earnestly hope that comrades will uphold their original aspirations, exert their remaining courage, and take swift action to condemn and punish them. Only then can all obstacles be removed, peace be permanently maintained, and the future of the nation truly depend on it.

The Shanghai Special City Executive Committee of the Chinese Kuomintang

Qi

▲Reply to Deputy Commander Zhang by Telegram To Deputy Commander Zhang Xueliang, Beiping,

We have just received your telegram advocating for weighing the advantages and disadvantages and saving the nation from danger. Your benevolent words are widely beneficial and deeply admired. At this time when the country is in danger of being destroyed and the people are in pain of being submerged, cutting our hair and putting on our armor is still insufficient. What is the intention of observing soldiers and flaunting military power? Even if it is said to be patriotism, the country should be the premise. If it is to save the people, the people should be the mission. If the fratricide cannot resist foreign aggression and the people in the same room only know how to wield swords, it is patriotism in name but harming the country in reality, and saving the people in the beginning but harming the people in the end. There is absolutely no way to succeed by harming the country and harming the people through perverse acts. As for political views that occasionally differ and personnel matters that are not without remedy, the party has discipline and the country has laws. By using laws and discipline to restrain each other, what disputes are there to speak of? If we disregard the national economy and the people's livelihood and only seek to resolve old grievances, it is tantamount to cutting ourselves off from the country and abandoning ourselves to the people. There is no way to survive if we cut ourselves off from the country and abandon ourselves to the people. Moreover, the melons of Huangtai are picked again and again, and there is no complete egg under the overturned nest. It is advisable to move the firewood early to prevent a fire. We hope that you will thoroughly implement your proposals, promote harmony, and the national interest and the people's happiness will depend on it.

The Shanghai Special City Executive Committee of the Chinese Kuomintang

Jia

Yesterday's Disaster Relief News from Various Provinces 120

More Disaster Victims Arrive in Shanghai

The Shanghai Disaster Victim Reception Center in Nanshi has completely vacated the guild halls and temples in Nanshi where disaster victims were staying in Shanghai and merged them all into the Chao Hui Villa and Qu Zhenren Temple. Yesterday, some Hubei and Gao Shao disaster victims stranded in Shanghai reported to the center, as they did not know about the reception center after arriving in Shanghai. There were 14 disaster victims from Hankou, Gaoyou, and Shaobo. The center arranged to accommodate them all in the Chao Hui Villa.

Yesterday afternoon at 7:00 PM, a train from Wuxi brought 32 refugees from Jiujiang. Leader Yu Shunbai reported to the 5th District Public Security Bureau and temporarily stayed in the district before going to Hangzhou.

Jiangsu Flood Relief Association News 121

▲Disaster Survey Report: Mr. Liu Cheng, a disaster survey specialist from the association, reported on the disaster situation in Liyang as follows: (Disaster Area) The county is low-lying with no water storage areas. Approximately 700,000 mu of farmland were affected, accounting for eight-tenths of the county's total land. (Disaster Victims) Thousands of people were displaced and fled to other towns or sought work as laborers in various cities. More than 2,000 people died. (Post-Disaster) Although the water has gradually receded, the low-lying areas still resemble vast rivers and lakes. In particular, Yuan Wan in District 2, Gu Du Lanxi in District 7, and Hutang Langwei in District 8 are like cauldrons, with the deepest water. Residents, young and old, are crying from hunger and cold, and those entering the city awaiting relief are constantly on the road. Even in higher areas, the crops have almost completely rotted, making replanting impossible. The collapsed houses and injured people along the breached dikes are too numerous to count. (Cause of Disaster) Since summer, there has been continuous rain and subsequent hurricanes. Mountain floods erupted, and river water rose sharply. Embanked and tidal farmland were successively submerged. (Spring Harvest) The total harvest for the entire county is estimated at only 22%.

▲Summary of Telegrams from Various Offices: Zhu Zhongjian in Gaoyou telegraphed that he has been rescuing more than 1,000 refugees daily. Among them, eight-tenths are willing to move south, and two-tenths are being accommodated. The post office is overcrowded with people staying overnight and eating, and rice, flour, and boats are insufficient. He requested that they be dispatched quickly. Cao Songqiao and Yuan Xiaogu in Yangzhou telegraphed that five shelters have been set up and are full, making it difficult to accommodate more people. Many more people are coming, so please quickly find a solution and another location. Hua Fuxian in Sishui telegraphed that 800 refugees have been sheltered up to the fishing day. He also telegraphed that 1,000 people are sheltered in Yanggeng, and those who want to leave are dismissed, with 600 people actually sheltered, mostly women and children.

▲Summary of Telegrams from Various Counties and Organizations: Gao Henian in Xinghua telegraphed that the Gao Shao Dike has breached, turning the eastern part of Taizhou, Xinghua, Yancheng, and Funing into a watery expanse, especially Xinghua. The water level has stopped rising and is increasing. He has urgently telegraphed the provincial government to quickly block the breach. Li Yushu in Huaiyin telegraphed that the disaster area in Huai's Siyang is vast, and there are many disaster victims. The Jisheng Society's relief funds are insufficient to distribute. He urgently requests further arrangements to dispatch personnel and relief supplies, preferably No. 4 or 5 flour, requiring 10,000 bags per county with strict inspection and generous distribution. Jiang Zhongxiang in Nanjing telegraphed that the Pu Zhen (Pukou relief) has been allocated 10,000 yuan, and a local meeting will be convened immediately to proceed. The Ning Yu Zhen (Ning Yu relief) is actively raising funds, and a detailed telegram will follow. Zhang Suijing in Yangzhou telegraphed that he received a letter instructing the allocation of 10,000 yuan for the purchase of 5,000 bags of flour, which have been shipped to Zhenjiang. He is grateful, but requests that the Yangzhou government send personnel to distribute it, as they are unfamiliar with the area and it is inconvenient. He still requests the association to take charge of the matter.

▲Continued Reports of Disaster Conditions from Various Counties: The magistrate of Yancheng County telegraphed that the water level in Yancheng rose sharply by two feet in two days, with the water depth in the plains exceeding ten feet. Except for a small area in the city, almost the entire county, hundreds of miles, is submerged. They are currently accommodating refugees separately and have dispatched committee members to provide relief in various townships. He urgently requests five steamships and a telegraphic transfer of 40,000 to 50,000 yuan for relief to save lives. Dai Hanwen in Funing telegraphed that the water depth in the plains in the southeast townships of Funing County is three to four feet, and it is still rising rapidly, with dire consequences. Furthermore, the old Yellow River dikes at the Meng and Er locations in the north of the county have also collapsed, inundating a significant amount of farmland and houses. They are currently accommodating and providing relief, but the disaster is severe and the relief is meager. He still requests a substantial increase in funds to save the disaster victims. The Dongtai Qian Budian Tobacco and South Goods Trade Association telegraphed that the Yun Dike has breached, causing the city to rise three feet, with water on all sides, halting all industries. The situation in the countryside, where houses are submerged, is even more dire. Millions of disaster victims are crying out for food. The relief funds allocated are a drop in the bucket. They urgently plead for a large amount of grain and funds to save the survivors. Han Xiyu, Ling Dichun, and others, difficult refugees in Taixian, stated that the water level is approaching the city day by day. They have blocked the Xin Guan (New Customs) North Gate, and the remaining gates and water gates are being prepared for blocking. The city is overcrowded, and food is running out. They heard that another five or six feet of water is coming, causing several alarms every night. In the four rural areas, cooking smoke has ceased, the sound of chickens and dogs is unheard, houses are drifting away, and the stench of floating corpses is unbearable. The relief funds issued by the province have long been exhausted. If funds are not continuously allocated, those who have been saved will eventually die.

▲Association Affairs News: The association originally scheduled a meeting of the entire executive committee for the 10th of this month. It has been learned that due to a conflict in time and location with the Fundraising Association for the Flood Disaster in Various Provinces, it has been changed to 4:00 PM on the 11th. All executive committee and standing committee members have been notified separately. Qiao Baoyuan, the association's disaster survey specialist and director of the Tongshan Emergency Relief, arrived in Shanghai on the Beijing-Shanghai train yesterday afternoon to discuss various relief matters. It is heard that Mr. Qiao's health has not yet recovered, and he looks very thin. His voice is also weak. The Jiangsu Association of Fellow Provincials in Beijing organized the Flood Disaster Emergency Relief Association and appointed Wu Jingheng, Niu Yongjian, Sun Bowen, and Zhang Yiou as standing committee members and representatives to come to Shanghai for discussions. Mr. Sun Bowen arrived at the association yesterday with official documents for consultation. It is heard that Mr. Wu, Niu, and Zhang will also arrive in Shanghai successively.

Jisheng Society's Handling of Jiangsu Relief 122

The Chinese Jisheng Society, given the unprecedented disaster this time, has promised to do its best in all severely affected areas and will promptly appoint directors to go for relief. The flood disaster in Jiangsu Province is no less severe than in Wuhan, such as Gaoyou and Shaobo, which are indeed unprecedented tragedies. The association publicly appointed Committee Member Zhang Xianqing, along with relief friends, to carry 30,000 yuan and 15,000 bags of flour. In addition, 2,000 bags were shipped from the Zhenjiang Yicheng Factory, totaling 17,000 bags. More will be shipped afterward, along with 32 boxes of biscuits and 6 boxes of relief medicine. Due to the extraordinarily severe disaster situation, Relief Friends Mu Jialiang and Sun Yinting were added to assist in handling the matter. For Huaiyin, Huaian, and Siyang counties, the society publicly appointed Zhou Yuankai and Li Yushu, the president and vice president of the Qingjiang Jisheng Branch, along with relief friends, to handle the distribution. The association allocated and remitted 20,000 yuan for relief, which was transferred to Qingjiang Yichang Zhuang through Dade Zhuang the day before yesterday. Five thousand bags of flour were also shipped in batches for relief. Reports continued to come from Xinghua, Dongtai, Yancheng, and other places, indicating that the disaster situation was even more severe. The society is currently lacking both personnel and funds, and although they have the desire to save people, they can only lament helplessly.

Gaoyou Refugees Cry Out the Reasons for the Disaster 123

Elders and fathers throughout the country, please be aware: Gaoyou has suffered from continuous rain this summer, and the suffering of farmers in low-lying areas has been extreme. As the Yi and Huai rivers rose and flowed into Gaobao Lake, the canal level reached 1 zhang 8 chi 7 cun. The dams were released to discharge water into the sea, and our county bore the brunt. All the embankments in the county were submerged. Agricultural products flowered but did not bear fruit, and tens of thousands of people died. Fortunately, the urban area could somewhat accommodate refugees. After autumn, the canal water level dropped slightly, and it was said that a part of the urban area had barely escaped with their lives. Who would have expected that on August 25th, a hurricane roared, and the water surged. At dusk, the city was flooded. The authorities were unable to take emergency measures and resorted to digging a well when thirsty. The loose soil could not withstand the water pressure, causing breaches in critical locations successively from 3:00 AM to 5:00 AM on August 26th, from Dangjun Tower in the north to Qigong Temple in the south, a length of about two li. The two sections in the middle that did not collapse were only about ten or twenty zhang each, forming isolated islands. The area outside the North Gate became a watery expanse, houses drifted, and countless old and young, men and women, drowned in the water. Corpses floated everywhere, almost like mountains. Those who were fortunate enough not to drown either climbed onto rooftops or treetops for help, or went to high ground or mounds to await rescue. The sound of crying corresponded to the sound of waves, a sight unbearable to see and a sound unbearable to hear. The urban area relied on the city walls for protection. This time, the city river water gate and the dam heads were weakly constructed and could not withstand the flood, causing backflow. Survivors are exposed to the elements and eating in the wind, becoming emaciated from starvation. The people of Gaoyou are innocent and have suffered this great calamity. Recalling the time of embankment protection, the provincial order instructed all water conservancy bureaus and county governments in the province to raise the subsidiary embankments by three chi. If the new embankment was strongly constructed and the materials were solid, it would have been able to withstand the floods. If the authorities had been responsible and conscientious, it would not have been difficult to eliminate the danger. However, the water conservancy bureau turned a blind eye and was unwilling to act, relying only on a small amount of silver collected by a certain chamber of commerce as a temporary fix. Although it is said to be a natural disaster, it was caused by humans. This is the first cause of the tragedy due to negligence. This year's flood disaster required a huge amount of expenditure. Blocking the downstream river and river mouth dam heads cost more than 4,400 yuan but still resulted in danger, requiring another 10,000 yuan for rescue. Blocking the Wanlv An Shuangmiao Diaoyugou three dams in the downstream required more than 12,200 yuan, which is not included in the previous expenditure. After the three dams in the upstream were blocked, the government was reluctant to spend money and perfunctorily increased the embankments, even shifting responsibility, so that the initiator was realistic and did not waste money when work began. How could it have reached the point where they were exhausted and had no rice to cook during the emergency rescue? This is the second cause of the tragedy due to dereliction of duty. Since the Republic, the spring repairs have always been funded with 800 yuan, which was already insufficient. This year, the deadline was missed, and only 5,000 yuan was issued. The bureau chiefs did not consider the importance of the matter and only issued money. According to records, during the Kangxi period of the Qing Dynasty, the Lotus Pond breached, and the city was surrounded by water, with the water only three chi from the city wall, yet the city was safe. This year, the blocking of the water gate and city gate was assigned to the government, with more funds than in the past, but the officials embezzled and enriched themselves, so that when the water reached the water gate, it immediately collapsed. This is the third cause of the tragedy due to corruption. Please investigate the causes of the disaster and punish the responsible persons according to the regulations of river affairs to serve as a warning for the future. This is what the helpless disaster victims hope from the national government and authorities. A tearful plea from the flood victims of Gaoyou County.

Xinghua Fellow Provincials Association Begs for Relief 124

The Xinghua Fellow Provincials Association sent a letter to various charitable organizations in Shanghai to beg for relief, stating: Respected sirs, the land has sunk in a great calamity, a severe disaster in Xinghua. The area is remote, and news is cut off, so the situation is not known outside. According to refugees who have fled to Shanghai, weeping and wailing, the severity of the disaster is rarely seen in history books, and the urgency of the need for rescue cannot be described in words. Now, we will describe the actual situation of the disaster to your association in detail. Our county has frequent floods and droughts, and famines have continued for years. The people's livelihood has been declining for years. Since the flood disaster in 1921, the vitality has not yet recovered. In 1928 and 1929, drought and salinity overlapped, and 200,000 strong men went to seek a living elsewhere. Last year's autumn harvest was only 30% to 40%. The water village is not suitable for growing wheat, and the spring crop is very small. The only thing they hoped for was the autumn harvest. This year, from May 14th, it rained heavily, non-stop for more than ten days. Before the disaster in the Huai River, the ditches were already overflowing, and half of the fields had been flooded. Then, the Huai River rose sharply, and all three dams were opened. The water depth in the plains reached ten feet, and all the fields in the entire territory were submerged. It was five days before the autumn harvest. According to the custom in this area, early rice starts to turn yellow at the beginning of autumn. The green rice is not yet ripe, and even harvesting it would be useless. Thus, a year's hard work was completely ruined by the flood. The entire territory has 4 million mu of good farmland, and the harvest from each mu is worth about 20 yuan, totaling a loss of nearly 80 million yuan. The livelihood of 600,000 people is on the verge of extinction. The water continues to rise daily, and the houses are also several feet under water. The villages in the four rural areas are building new embankments to defend against the flood. Who would have expected that on the afternoon of August 26th, the Post and Shao dams breached, as if pouring the water of three lakes to sink a leaky boat? When the water reached Xinghua, the people of Xinghua were still dreaming. The water surged and rose several feet in an instant. Furthermore, the wind was strong, and the rain was heavy. The village embankments in the four rural areas collapsed by the hundreds and thousands. There were survivors clinging to tree tops and rooftops, and drowned ghosts of women and children floating in the waves. The sound of crying shook the sky and did not cease for hundreds of miles. The next day, when the water stabilized somewhat, those whose houses had collapsed immediately dismantled the pillars to nail piles, trying to reinforce and block desperately. But they could not succeed, and entire villages boarded boats. Before the Post and Shao dams breached, the Lao Embankment, Zhong Embankment, Yongfeng Embankment, and Heta Embankment in the northeast, as well as the Lao Embankment, Sanjiao Embankment, and Fire Dragon Embankment connecting to the damaged Yancheng, were still in good condition, although the water was close to the top of the embankment. The early rice had also been harvested. After the breach, the wind carried the water and surged, making it impossible to protect them, and they collapsed one after another. Houses, livestock, and newly harvested early rice were all swept away. From then on, in Xinghua, for more than a hundred li in all directions, there was not a single piece of dry land. The county seat, the highest point, was also half-submerged in water. Most of the houses outside the city were washed away. The only thing they relied on was a lone city wall. To this day, the breach in the Yun Embankment has not yet been completely blocked, and the water level continues to rise by two or three inches every day. If this continues to accumulate, even this lone city will be submerged, which is only a matter of time. In this Jianghuai flood disaster, apart from Post and Shao being the most directly affected, Xingtai, Dongtai, Yancheng, and Funing are the most severely affected among the five counties. Among the five counties, Xinghua is the most severely affected because it is adjacent to Gaoyou and was flooded first. The terrain is the lowest, the water is deepest, the downstream drainage is poor, the water storage is the widest, and the water recedes the slowest. In the past, there was a saying that Hong Lake moved east, and now it has come true. Xinghua has completely become the bottom of the lake, while other counties are still on the edge of the lake. When winter arrives, the starving will have no food, and the cold will have no clothing. If hundreds of thousands of disaster victims barely clinging to life are not provided with relief, they will all die afterward. In previous famine years, farmers went to Jiangnan to find food. This year, Suzhou, Changzhou, Jiaxing, and Huzhou are also severely affected by the disaster. Now, even this place to find food is no longer available. The old and weak are sitting and waiting to die, while the strong are taking risks. Those who do not die from water will die from hunger, and those who do not die from hunger will die from robbery. The difficulties ahead are unimaginable. Since the breach, although we have received assistance from various sectors, the amount received is limited, like adding wood to a burning fire or dripping water on a burning mountain. The people are suffering more from the burning. We look north to the clouds, our souls fly away, and our intestines are broken. We use these urgent words to beg your association to increase the allocation of relief funds to relieve the suffering of those on the verge of death and save the lives of those about to drown. The Xinghua Fellow Provincials Association kowtows.

Dongtai Fellow Provincials Report Disaster Conditions 125

The Dongtai Fellow Provincials Association in Shanghai received news of the Dongtai flood disaster yesterday. At present, the relatively high urban area is besieged by floodwaters. Houses near the river are completely submerged, with depths of seven or eight feet. Even the highest county government front gate and second gate are flooded, so another back door has been opened on Main Street (Dongtai Main Street, which spans the Fan Embankment) to facilitate entry and exit. Main streets such as He Duo, Sanli Bridge, Magong Bridge, Xinba, and Caiyi Street are a foot deep in water. In the past, these were the most prosperous commercial areas, with a constant stream of pedestrians. Now, they are unusually deserted. The area near the North and South City Roots, Lujiatan, and the rural areas where refugees have come to the city are all borrowing ancient temples for accommodation. The number of arrivals increases daily, making it difficult to accommodate them, and there is a risk of starvation. However, many relief organizations have not yet arrived. We hope that all relief officials will pay special attention, knowing that saving from water is like saving from fire.

China Foreign Famine Relief Commission Disaster Relief Work 126

▲Overseas Chinese Enthusiastically Contribute: Overseas Chinese in various places are concerned about the flood disaster in their homeland and have constantly remitted large sums of money to Shanghai. Yesterday, the China Foreign Famine Relief Commission received (1) 10,000 yuan in foreign currency remitted by overseas Chinese in Surabaya, Java; (2) 2,000 taels of silver remitted by overseas Chinese in Semarang; (3) 80 pounds in English gold remitted by overseas Chinese in Shetland.

▲Xu Wenzhao Uses Award Money to Help Relief: The Western Medicine Department of the Lao Jinlong Foreign Company advertised for slogans for Yan Yisheng's Red Blood Pills and Tonic Pills. The first prize was 100 yuan, which was won by Mr. Xu Wenzhao of the Shanghai Central Trust Company. Mr. Xu immediately donated the award money to the China Foreign Famine Relief Commission to be used for flood relief in various places. Furthermore, the members of the Shanghai Cotton Cloth Trade Association, Yuchun Fengji, raised 2,500 yuan in foreign currency from the Luan Chang Company, which was also sent to the commission yesterday for relief.

▲Xinghua Branch Reports on Work: Yesterday, the commission received a report from the Xinghua Branch stating that Xinghua is shaped like a cauldron, and the disaster situation is extremely severe. The branch is currently distributing bread and flour to the most distressed areas and is building straw sheds on streets in the city without water to accommodate disaster victims. However, most of the streets are knee-deep in water, making the work very difficult. In the water-affected areas outside Xinghua City, disaster victims are still gathering on rooftops, and there is a risk of collapse at any time, which means that these people will be buried in the bellies of fish. However, these disaster victims are still attached to their homeland and do not want to leave. It is predicted that the water will not recede completely until at least three months later, so the idea of replanting is a pipe dream. By that time, it will already be winter, and the suffering of disaster victims from hunger and cold is only just beginning.

Continued Reports of Flood Disasters in Various Counties of Anhui 127

▲Wuhu: The entire county is a vast expanse of water, with a water depth of eight feet in the plains. Boats travel through the streets, and dozens of houses collapse every day. Many people and livestock have been washed away by the water. The disaster situation is extremely severe, and hundreds of thousands of people in the entire county are crying out for food.

▲Tongling: All 96 embankments and 13 islands in the entire county (totaling tens of thousands of mu of farmland) have been breached. The number of people and livestock that have been washed away is countless. In the village of Beigeng alone, hundreds of people have drowned. The total number of disaster victims in the county is 170,000.

▲Huaining: Hundreds of embankments in Guangcheng Embankment, Haikou Island, Badu Lake, and other places have collapsed successively, covering a length of 200 li. More than 1,000 people have died, and more than 10,000 livestock have been washed away. More than 100,000 disaster victims have no clothing or food.

▲Guichi: Embankments, fields, villages, and houses have been completely submerged. The number of people and livestock buried in the bellies of fish is unknown. Hundreds of thousands of disaster victims gather in high mountains and hills, using tree bark and grass roots to replace grain for hunger.

▲Fanchang: Embankments and dikes in the entire county have been breached, affecting 190,000 mu. Houses have collapsed completely, and more than 90,000 people are displaced. More than 200,000 people have no clothing or food.

▲Nanling: Large and small embankments have collapsed one after another. More than 100,000 disaster victims have no clothing or food and are on the verge of death.

▲Bengbu: The entire city is eight feet deep in water. Houses have collapsed, accounting for nine-tenths of the entire city. Disaster victims gather on the mountains to live.

Page 14

▲Susong: Dikes and embankments have been breached by hundreds of zhang. The water depth in the plains is more than ten feet. The disaster situation in the southeast is even more severe, with more than 300,000 disaster victims.

▲Wangjiang: More than 60 embankments along the banks have collapsed successively. Houses that have collapsed account for seven-tenths of the entire county. The number of people, livestock, and equipment washed away by the waves is countless.

I have complied with the instructions. After the funds were remitted, I, along with the Tianjin funds, handed them over to the Yingshang County government to entrust Mr. Yu Youquan in Bengbu, who is from Yingshang, to remit them to Yingshang, and then accompanied relief friends to distribute them in Yingshang and Wuhe. Xu Guozhi kowtows, tiny.

There are more arrivals, and emergency relief must take into account both local people and those crossing the border to start. It is difficult to organize without requesting an additional allocation of 20,000 yuan. Liu Lingsheng kowtows, sings.

The disaster situation in Anhui has been requested by relief friends to investigate and meet in Bengbu around the fishing day to distribute funds. All Sectors Enthusiastically Help Relief 129

▲Xiang Songmao Helps Raise More Than 10,000 Yuan: Mr. Xiang Songmao, General Manager of the Wuzhou Pharmacy, initiated business-assisted relief. In addition to the Wuzhou and Taihe Pharmacies donating more than 5,000 yuan, Mr. Xiang also exhausted his personal abilities to solicit donations from various parties, including more than 2,000 yuan from the shareholders of the Yu Sheng Manganese Mine Company and more than 300 yuan from the colleagues of the Zhonghua Steel Company. As of yesterday, he had raised more than 5,000 yuan in foreign currency, totaling more than 10,000 yuan, which has been recorded and submitted to the relief association for distribution.

▲Bean and Rice Industry Donates 1,000 Bags of Flour: The Bean and Rice Trade Association donated flour to help the flood disaster in northern Jiangsu. Yesterday, they sent a letter to Magistrate Wang of Gaoyou County, stating that our association, not shirking our meager contribution, has raised 1,000 bags of flour and arranged for shipment to assist in emergency relief. We earnestly request the magistrate to inspect and promptly distribute them.

▲Marine Engineers' Flood Relief Association Established: The China Federation of Marine Engineers held a Flood Relief Association yesterday. Xu Linxun, Lin Jiazhou, Wang Qingfeng, Zhang Wenxing, Zhang Guixuan, Li Liansheng, Li Yuncheng, Sun Xinfen, and 50 other people attended. Xu Linxun was publicly elected as chairman. A ceremony was held, and the meeting elected (3) Xu Linxun, Lin Jiazhou, Wang Qingfeng, and Li Liansheng as executive committee members; (4) Xu Linxun and Lin Jiazhou as standing committee members for relief; (5) Sun Xin was appointed as the captain of the fundraising team to command the team members; (6) eight team members were assigned and divided into two teams; (7) fundraising members will solicit donations from marine engineers daily after receiving the donation register; (8) the donated funds will be submitted to the standing committee members daily for storage in a designated bank; (9) the fundraising period is tentatively set for three months; (10) no fundraising is allowed along the road; (11) the names of the donors will be published in the newspaper after the fundraising is completed.

▲30,000 Street Vendors in Shanghai Rise Up to Join Forces for Relief: Street vendors Liu Bingfu, Bao Lianqing, Tu Yunliang, Li Dongsheng, and others organized the Shanghai Jiang Municipal Street Vendor Industry Savings Association in 1924, with no less than several thousand members. Together with non-member colleagues in Shanghai, there are approximately 30,000 people. Due to the extraordinarily severe national flood disaster this time, and neighboring countries have also contributed funds for relief, although street vendors are small businesses, but for the sake of compatriots, they cannot bear to sit idly by. Therefore, the original initiators Tang Xiaobao and others invited colleagues to discuss and decided to jointly unite all street vendors in Shanghai to donate as much as possible, and appointed representatives to consult Yu Qiaqing, Fang Jiaobo, and others for support. On one hand, the initiators will strictly organize and establish sound measures, and separately order donation registers, affixing seals, and assign honest street vendors to solicit donations at various vegetable markets. The donation collectors will issue receipts and submit them daily to Liu Bingfu of Taihe Fish Market on Xiaodongmen Main Street for safekeeping. When the amount has accumulated, it will be transferred to the Emergency Relief Associations of various provinces and remitted to the disaster areas, and the initiators will publish a statement in the newspaper to ensure transparency.

▲Zhongnan Hotel Staff Donates 200 Yuan: At the Zhongnan Hotel at Dongxin Bridge, Mr. Lu Liankui and Mr. Li Wencai enthusiastically initiated a donation from the hotel staff, raising 200 yuan in foreign currency for disaster relief, which has now been delivered to the relief agency for distribution.

Chu Minyi Returned to Shanghai Yesterday 132

The French Delegation Still Remains in the Provincial Capital of Xinjiang

The True Situation of the Sino-French Dispute

A Detailed Report Will Be Given in Beijing Soon

He Will Return to His Ancestral Home Next Week to Attend the Funeral

Mr. Chu Minyi, a member of the Central Committee, was previously dispatched by the Central Government to Xinjiang to investigate party affairs and also served as the head of the Chinese side of the Sino-French Academic Investigation Team. He went to various places in the Northwest for on-the-spot investigations. Unfortunately, a dispute occurred midway, and the National Government ordered the cessation of the investigation. After receiving the order in Dihua, Mr. Chu immediately returned to China via Russia, taking the China Eastern Railway southward. He arrived in Shanghai by overnight express train from Beijing yesterday morning. Our reporter interviewed him at the Sino-French Industrial School yesterday. Mr. Chu looked grief-stricken due to mourning his father, and travel-worn, but his spirits were still very high. According to Mr. Chu,

▲Attending the Report

I (Chu, referring to himself) arrived in Beijing yesterday morning (i.e., the morning before yesterday), stayed for half a day, and did not meet with Chairman Chiang. I took a train back to Shanghai that evening to take care of school and family matters. I plan to go to Beijing next Monday to attend the Central Party Headquarters' Memorial Week and report in detail the whole story of the dispute of the Sino-French Investigation Team, etc. Yesterday, Chu sent a telegram to the Central Government, saying: "To the Secretariat of the Central Party Headquarters in Nanjing, for the information of all committee members, Minyi was ordered to go to Xinjiang and has now completed the inspection. I left Dihua on the 11th of last month and returned to Shanghai via Russia to attend the funeral. As soon as family and school matters are settled, I will come to Beijing to report on the inspection situation. Furthermore, the dispute in the Sino-French Academic Team during the journey has caused many misunderstandings due to the delay in letters and telegrams. In addition to the report already made to the Antiquities Preservation Committee in Beiping, it is still necessary to make a supplementary explanation in person. I hereby report this in advance. Chu Minyi respectfully bows."

▲Achievements of the Crawling Vehicles

Mr. Chu then said that the Sino-French Scientific Investigation Team of 1920 was divided into East and West teams to enter Xinjiang. The West Team was entirely organized by the French, entering Xinjiang via Asia Minor, with Mr. Halde as the head. The East Team, i.e., my team, was a joint team of Chinese and French, with myself as the Chinese team leader and Mr. Bouan, the assailant, as the French team leader. We departed from Beiping, passing through Xi'an, Lanzhou, Suzhou, and Hami, and arrived in Dihua, totaling five legs, each with 18 stations, each station being approximately 90 li. Normally, each station would take a day to travel. It should have taken four months from Zhangjiakou to Dihua, but because we used crawling vehicles, we departed from Zhangjiakou on May 17th and arrived in Dihua on July 7th, taking only 50 days. Excluding the 15 days of delay on the way, it actually took 35 days, truly opening a new era in Xinjiang transportation.

▲Advantages and Disadvantages of the Crawling Vehicles

However, the crawling vehicles have both advantages and disadvantages. The advantage is that the wheels do not sink in when driving in the desert, allowing for free movement. The disadvantage is that the speed is too slow when driving inland. I have drafted an improvement plan for the future development of Xinjiang transportation.

▲The Reality of the Dispute

As for the course of this dispute, the French team leader, Mr. Bouan, acted improperly and even beat our team member, Hao Jingsheng. At that time, the Chinese team members were very angry and gathered in Suzhou on June 15th to negotiate with the French side and requested the local government to stop the investigation. At that time, Mr. Hao and Mr. Zhou and Mr. Han had already withdrawn. However, our side also telegraphed the National Government to report, but the telegram arrived too late, causing misunderstandings among the people in the mainland. In fact, at that time, we were also unwilling to cooperate with the French side. Later, with the mediation of Ma Hongbin, the chairman of the 20 provinces, we signed seven conditions with the French side (i.e., the removal of Bouan and other seven conditions) before continuing the journey. We left Suzhou on June 21st, traveled west, arrived in Hami, Xinjiang Province on June 27th, arrived in Turpan on July 5th, and arrived in Dihua on July 7th, where we received the first order from the National Government to stop the investigation. Soon after, we received an order to prohibit the investigation and protect the French team members. We immediately obeyed the order and stopped the investigation. I and the Chinese team members then departed from Russia and returned to China. This trip covered more than 25,000 li. Although the dispute caused an impact, the investigation results and images seen were excellent.

▲The French Delegation Stays in Xinjiang

The reason why the Chinese delegation returned first and the French delegation remained in Xinjiang Province is that the French side had to wait for the arrival of the West Team before returning to China. However, investigations are now prohibited in Xinjiang Province. Beforehand, the Xinjiang Provincial Government originally planned to order the French delegation to stay in Turpan temporarily. Later, due to Bouan's repeated requests, they were allowed to stay in Dihua. Bouan also sent a letter of apology to the Xinjiang Provincial Government, which has not been published by any newspapers. The following is a transcript: "(To Chairman, with respect, this letter is to inform you that during the desert trip of our delegation, Bouan had a conflict with Mr. Hao Jingsheng, a member of your delegation, over trivial matters, which led to reckless use of force. After thinking about it, I feel very inappropriate. Last night, Your Excellency ordered Bouan to stay in the provincial capital pending orders. Due to my impatience, I wanted to leave without thinking, which was extremely absurd. Bouan is young and inexperienced. In addition, I am carrying the mission of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs of our country. The people who came with me between staying in Turpan were visiting your country for the first time. I felt uneasy about abandoning them in the hot city of Turpan. Dr. Chu Minyi and General Yao Xijiu had many acquaintances among my friends and relatives in our country. They know Bouan's personality better. Therefore, I hope that Your Excellency will be extra lenient on the above two major mistakes and temporarily allow Bouan to stay with the members of our delegation in Turpan to await your orders. If this is approved, please send someone to accompany the vehicle, and Bouan will never dare to take any improper actions.)"

▲One Member of the Chinese Delegation

The entire Chinese delegation had a total of eight people. Except for Mr. Hao and the other two who withdrew midway, there were six people who arrived in Dihua. I and the other five returned together. Only Mr. Liu Shenchan, a botanist sent by the Academia Sinica, decided to stay longer for more investigation because it was not easy to reach Xinjiang. Therefore, only one member of the Chinese delegation remained in Xinjiang.

▲Northwest Transportation

After this investigation, we have a general understanding of the situation in the Northwest. In terms of party affairs, although the Central Government has not officially recognized it, there is a lot of party work and the dissemination of the Three Principles of the People has been going on for a long time. In terms of society, the people can be said to be extremely simple and honest. In terms of politics, the organization of the Xinjiang Provincial Government is the same as the central establishment, with four departments for civil affairs, finance, construction, and education, and a secretary-general. However, since the establishment of the provincial government, there has never been a provincial government meeting, which is somewhat different from other places. The most important thing is transportation, and Russia's attempt to invade Xinjiang is particularly worrying. The transportation between Xinjiang Province and the mainland is extremely obstructed. Usually, all exports are made by Russia, which leads to Russia's monopoly. Now, Soviet Russia is planning a railway branch line from Ayakoz of the Turkestan–Siberia Railway to Tacheng. Once completed, it will be a matter of arrival in the evening after departure in the morning. Not only will the southern industry be completely absorbed, but the border issue is also worrying. At present, to save everything in Xinjiang, we must start by opening up transportation. In the past, there were three routes from the country to Xinjiang: one from Suiyuan to Guchengzi, which is the shortest, only taking seventy or eighty days, but it is very dangerous because it passes through the desert; one from Beiping to Hami, passing through Xi'an, Lanzhou, and Suzhou, totaling five stations, each taking eighteen days, and it takes ninety days to arrive. This route has a denser population and is more convenient for travelers; and another route from Yangguan Avenue to Has, which takes one hundred and twenty days, which is the slowest.

▲Returning to His Ancestral Home for the Funeral

Mr. Chu plans to attend the Memorial Week in Beijing to report and then return to his ancestral home in Huzhou to attend the funeral and choose a date for the memorial service. There are no actions of any kind planned in Beijing or Shanghai.

The British Merchant's Public Bus Labor Strike Still Has No Solution 134

The Company Sends Police to Protect the Buses

And Refuses Unconditional Resumption of Work

After the British merchant's public bus workers went on strike again, the situation is quite serious. The public buses that are barely running are protected by armed Chinese police escorts. Yesterday, some workers were willing to resume work unconditionally, but were also refused. The various situations are recorded as follows:

▲Protecting the Buses

After the company announced the dismissal of all striking workers, the situation was quite serious. In order to prevent accidents, the company shortened the routes of Routes 1 and 9, which are barely running, moved the time of entering the factory earlier, and requested the police station to send armed Chinese police escorts. Yesterday, there were 12 buses running on Route 1, with the fare remaining the same; 8 buses on Route 2, with a uniform fare of 16 cents; 8 buses on Route 5, with a uniform fare of 11 cents; and 18 buses on Route 9, with a uniform fare of 20 cents. Each bus was protected by one armed Chinese policeman sent by the police station.

▲Refusing to Resume Work

After the British merchant's public bus strike committee put forward 11 conditions, which were rejected by the company, they declared that they would continue the strike and fight to the end, and would not resume work until their goals were achieved. Some workers, who were forced by livelihood, sent nine representatives to the main factory on Connaught Road yesterday morning to negotiate and were willing to resume work unconditionally. However, the chief manager, Gunther, refused to meet them, indicating his refusal. All the Chinese people in the company were filled with hatred for the unreasonable oppression of the foreigners.

▲Company's Plan

Since the public bus workers announced the strike on August 20, the company has lost more than 1,000 yuan every day. Of the 40 new workers recruited previously, only one-third passed the repeated training. Most of the newly recruited workers failed. The company plans to stop recruiting new workers and maintain the public buses on Routes 1, 2, 5, and 9 in a calm manner. It completely rejects any demands from the striking workers. Therefore, it is not easy for the public buses in the concession to fully recover for a while, and the labor strike is bound to be prolonged.

The Real Estate Association Recommends Xiao Qingyun to Join the Water Supply Investigation Committee 135

A Bumper Harvest of Autumn Cocoons is Expected 136

The Phenomenon of Lowering Prices to Collect Cocoons

The Pessimistic Future of the Silk Industry

In recent years, the silk and cocoon industry has been extremely depressed. Last year, due to the high price of cocoons and the low price of silk, silk factories suffered heavy losses and could not sustain themselves. They immediately appealed to the government to issue silk industry bonds to maintain them. However, the number of silk factories operating in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces this year is less than half of the total. This spring, silkworm eggs suffered severe damage from the weather, and cocoon production was extremely low. Silk mills hope that the autumn cocoons will make up for it. Fortunately, since the beginning of autumn, the temperature has been moderate, and those raising autumn silkworms in the Jiangsu and Zhejiang cocoon areas are very enthusiastic. Recently, they are about to mount the frames, and a bumper harvest is expected, especially in Wuxi and Wujin. Yesterday, we received reliable news from Wuxi that a small number of cocoons can be harvested in the northeast countryside, and the quality of the cocoons is still good. Silk and cocoon merchants are panicking and lowering prices to compete for collection. The price of fresh cocoons has been lowered to more than 70 yuan per picul. The cost of raw silk is more than 1,000 taels of silver per bale of 100 catties. According to the current price of silk, each bale will lose 100 to 200 taels of silver, which is really their own fault. Moreover, most are currently mounting the frames, so it is inevitable to avoid the disadvantages of picking tender cocoons (i.e., falling off the mountain early without waiting for the cocoons to mature). Therefore, the future of the silk mill industry is even more pessimistic.

Silk Industry Bonds Will Be Issued Soon 137

More Than 50 Silk Factories Have Resumed Operation

More Than 10,000 Workers are Saved From Unemployment Due to the Bonds

The 4 million yuan of the Jiang-Zhe Silk Industry Bonds, which are aimed at addressing the urgent issues, have been issued by the Fund Management Committee entrusted to the Guohuo Bank Trust Department since August 31. Silk manufacturers have been going to collect the bonds in succession in accordance with the procedures. As of yesterday, 95% have been collected. For example, 108 single-reeling factories and 7 double-reeling factories in Shanghai have all collected the bonds, except for the 7 double-reeling factories that have not collected them due to the customs collection of the fund. In Wuxi, 48 single-reeling factories have all collected the bonds, except for one that has not collected them. In Zhejiang, 25 single-reeling factories have only 4 that have not collected them. They can be fully issued within a few days. The silk factories that have received the bonds are all preparing to resume operation. For example, in this city, the number has increased from 36 to 52. More than 10,000 workers have jobs due to the bonds. The foreign bank silk market has turned around slightly. For example, the price of the 20-22 denier silk exported to the United States is 950 taels per picul for the first grade and 920 taels for the second grade. Therefore, it is expected that the number of silk factories resuming operation in this city can still increase within a few days.

Bureau of Social Affairs 138

Formulates Factory Inspection Plan

Divided into Five Steps

The Factory Inspection Law will be implemented on October 1. Whether the implementation is appropriate is of great importance to the future of our country's industry and the welfare of workers. Therefore, the Bureau of Social Affairs of this city has selected qualified personnel and sent them to the Factory Inspection Personnel Training Institute of the Ministry of Industry for training. The inspectors graduated on September 3 and have returned to the bureau for work on the 4th. The work plan has been formulated by the director of the inspection section of the bureau, Tian Heqing, and is divided into five steps: The first step is registration, which is to extract one by one the factories in this city that comply with the Factory Law, and then send a letter to the factory, setting a time limit for complying with the registration and reporting procedures. The second step is investigation, which is to have the inspectors formulate detailed forms and go to each factory to investigate the factory's equipment and the safety equipment for key personnel, mechanical safety equipment, and sanitation equipment in detail for reference. The third step is to formulate the minimum standard regulations for various equipment so that each factory has something to follow. The fourth step is to be responsible for persuasion and assistance, and the factories may also be assisted when necessary. The fifth step is to wait for the equipment of each factory to reach a considerable level before conducting inspections in accordance with the law. The bureau is currently carrying out preliminary work. On the 7th, it sent people to consult the forms investigated by the Industrial Joint Investigation Office of this city to make a preliminary design, extract the factories in this city that comply with the Factory Law, and then proceed with registration, investigation, and other work. In addition to the inspectors carrying out daily work, the bureau also organizes a Factory Equipment Review Committee to review all difficult issues. The committee held its first meeting yesterday to discuss the difficult issues in the Factory Law. The results have not been announced because the time is not right.
